Important Foreign Telegrams

London Conference Opens 53

Political Leaders from Seven Countries Gather in One Hall

A Major Turning Point in the European Economy

Speech by British Prime Minister MacDonald

Confidence in Investment in Germany

Said to Be Necessary to Restore

The United States Plans to Submit a Concrete New Plan

Advocates for Short-Term Loans to Germany

The Conference is Limited to Discussing Financial Matters and Does Not Include Disarmament

The International Court of Justice Begins to Examine the German-Austrian Tax Agreement

▲ Reuters, London, 20th: Officials from France, Germany, Italy, and Belgium arrived at Victoria Station in London tonight. Within an hour, they gathered in the Prime Minister's room in the British House of Commons, along with representatives from the United Kingdom, the United States, and Japan, for a preliminary meeting. The crowds gathered at the station and outside the House of Commons were quite dense, showing the importance that people generally attach to this seven-nation conference. The representatives of each country were greeted by the British Prime Minister, Foreign Minister, and Chancellor of the Exchequer and led into the room. The British Prime Minister gave an opening speech, outlining the situation that the meeting must deal with. French Prime Minister Laval reported on the proceedings of the meeting in Paris and explained the spirit of initiating talks between France and Germany. He also described in detail France's position in this matter and expressed the hope for faithful cooperation between France and Germany to restore world trust. German Chancellor Brüning also explained the spirit of cooperation, thanked him for the opportunity of the Paris talks, and gave a detailed account of Germany's financial situation and the measures taken to deal with it, repeatedly stating the need for assistance to Germany. Finally, the procedural issues were discussed, and it was decided to reconvene at the Foreign Office in the morning.

▲ Reuters, London, 20th: The executive meeting was held today for two hours. British Prime Minister MacDonald briefly stated the reasons for the German panic and the decline of world commerce. The Prime Minister said that President Hoover's proposal to suspend debt payments was an act of perseverance and political skill, and also a timely move. Germany's plight must be helped to avoid dragging down the whole of Europe. The confidence of investors in Germany must be restored. Of course, most of what can be done must be left to bankers and financiers, but the agreement of this meeting can restore trust and courage to the people of all countries. This meeting will become a pivot of fortune and misfortune in world history. If a solution to the current difficulties cannot be found, the political and financial dangers that will arise will be unpredictable. If a solution can be found, it will be a clear demonstration of the gradual effectiveness of international cooperation. The Prime Minister later had dinner with German Chancellor Brüning and Finance Minister Kortis in the House of Commons, with British Foreign Secretary Henderson and Chancellor of the Exchequer Snowden also in attendance. A full meeting of the executive meeting will be held at 10:00 am tomorrow.

▲ Reuters, Washington, 21st: Last night, Secretary of State Stimson telephoned President Hoover, saying that Prime Minister MacDonald's speech at the opening of the executive meeting was pleasant and friendly. The official arena then issued a message stating that the United States' proposed relief measures for Germany will be submitted to the London Conference today.

▲ Reuters, London, 21st: After discussing various matters this morning, the London Conference has been adjourned. U.S. Secretary of State Stimson announced at the meeting that the United States has not withdrawn any loans from Germany and has even increased the original amount. The general impression is that the result of this meeting will be to continue short-term loans and not to make new loans.

▲ National News Agency, London, 21st: British newspapers said that as a result of yesterday's talks between representatives of various countries, it seemed that the original plan for long-term loans to Germany had been abandoned and replaced by short-term loans due in October, and it was decided to adjourn the meeting until autumn for further consideration.

▲ National News Agency, Berlin, 20th: Although the center of Pan-European politics has shifted from Paris to London, the German people's concern for the Franco-German conference has not diminished, and the lack of concrete results from the conference has aroused public debate. Peace-oriented newspapers such as the Berliner Tageblatt and Germania all said that the actual effect of the Franco-German conference, whatever it is, cannot be ignored in terms of its historical value. The Börsen-Zeitung said that although the Franco-German conference lacked concrete results, France was able to acknowledge the existence of the German financial crisis and the urgency of relief, so there is still hope for previous actions. Opposition newspapers said that Germany is Germany, and France is France, and the Third Republic of France will always be hostile to Germany, just as a leopard will never lose its spots. The Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung called the Paris meeting hypocritical and advised the people not to be misled by excessive propaganda. After all, the French are a polite nation, and now that German politicians are visiting France, their sweet words and respectful etiquette are their diplomatic conventions. The newspaper cited as evidence the speech given by French Minister of War Maginot at a banquet for World War I sergeants in Montmédy on Sunday. At a time when the discussion of France's joining international organizations and the German financial relief plan was in full swing at the Franco-German conference, Maginot still strongly opposed it. Although German public opinion's opposition was very strong, the government remained silent. According to people in political circles, the Paris meeting was only a preliminary meeting, and the results will depend on the London Conference. Moreover, France has never made any government requests at the Paris meeting, and even Laval and Briand's visit to England has not been heard with any accompanying conditions.

▲ National News Agency, Washington, 20th: The London Daily News political correspondent said that the United States plans to ask France, Italy, and Germany to stop building warships for a year, or at least suspend them until after the Disarmament Conference next spring. This statement will be submitted by Stimson to the Seven-Nation Executive Conference tomorrow. Today, the U.S. Department of State denied this and solemnly stated that the main purpose of the United States' invitation to attend the Executive Conference is only to help an agreement to provide financial assistance to Germany.

▲ National News Agency, London, 20th: Although the Seven-Nation Executive Conference is limited to discussing the German financial problem, U.S. Secretary of State Stimson is still unofficially conducting disarmament issues here as the representative of the U.S. President. At 4:00 pm today, the Japanese Ambassador to the United Kingdom visited Mr. Stimson and talked for half an hour. It was heard that the Japanese Ambassador assured that Japan is ready to cooperate with the United States sincerely on the plan to suspend war debts, and had a brief discussion on the disarmament issue. Later, when Mr. Stimson and Mellon met with U.S. news reporters, they also said that they had talked with the Japanese Ambassador about disarmament, but Mr. Stimson did not say whether this was discussed during lunch with British Prime Minister MacDonald at the Hyde Park Hotel at noon.

▲ National News Agency, The Hague, 20th: The International Court of Justice held its 22nd special meeting here today, chaired by Japanese representative Adachi. The most important event on the agenda of this meeting is the German-Austrian tariff agreement, followed by the dispute between Denmark and Norway over the sovereignty of East Greenland. The meeting will last about a week, so the resolution on the German-Austrian tariff agreement will probably be released before the closing of the Seven-Nation Executive Conference in London.

Indian Round Table Conference Expanded 54

Leaders of the People's Party Invited to Participate

▲ Reuters, London, 21st: To expand the foundation of the Indian Round Table Conference and to include the leaders of the Indian National Congress Party, British Prime Minister MacDonald has issued 36 invitations to participate in the Federal Structure Committee meeting to be held in London in early September. Last year, a total of 21 representatives attended the Federal Structure Committee meeting. Now Gandhi is one of the newly invited members. Representatives of oppressed nationalities, workers, and women in India are also participating this time. The number of Muslim representatives has also increased. The date of the meeting has not yet been determined and is expected to be announced soon. The possibility of Gandhi coming to England reminds people of Gandhi's first visit to England forty-two years ago. At that time, Gandhi was 19 years old and entered university to study law. Later, he became a lawyer and resided in South Africa, witnessing the plight of overseas Chinese and thinking of ways to help them, and invented the theory of non-violent resistance. He returned to India before the European War, and during the war, he helped British officials recruit Indian soldiers.

Former U.S. Interior Secretary Jailed for Oil Bribery Case 55

▲ Reuters, Santa Fe, 21st: Fall, the former Secretary of the Interior, has been jailed for one year and one day today for oil bribery.

Important News

The Northeast After Shih Yiu-san’s Aberration 56

Chang Hsueh-liang Upholds Peaceful Principles

▲ One Side Hopes for Shih’s Awakening

▲ The Other Side Has Long Been Prepared

Tianjin Dispatch: The aberration of Shih Yiu-san’s 13th Route Army was already evident in late May and early June. On June 12th, the Northeast Army urgently dispatched three brigades of infantry and one brigade of artillery into the Shanhaiguan Pass. At that time, the situation between the two sides was almost at the point of ignition. The fact that it was delayed until now to erupt is due to Chang Hsueh-liang’s painstaking efforts to maintain peace in the North, which should be understood by the people of the country. Although there have been minor clashes, the Northeast peace envoys are still running around. It is unknown whether they can turn hostility into friendship. The beginning and end of the incident are described as follows:

▲ Instigation by Reactionaries: Shih Yiu-san’s mind is very simple. He often says to his subordinates in his speeches, "I don't understand what is called a doctrine. I only know that whoever gives me money to spend, I will work for him." Therefore, his personality is fickle. This is very obvious based on Shih's actions in recent years. After the failure of Yan and Feng last year, the Central Government originally intended to resolve Shih's troops, but Chang Hsueh-liang was generous and always remembered the word "peace," so he pleaded with the Central Government to incorporate them. However, he still felt that the monthly salary given by the Central Government was insufficient and often complained. The reactionaries then took the opportunity to use their divisive tactics, causing suspicion and alienation. In March, Shih went to Liaoning to ask Chang to urge the Central Government to remit the monthly salary. He stayed in Liaoning for a month. It was widely rumored that Shih was imprisoned. Although he safely returned to his defense, the rumors made Shih feel uneasy. Soon after, the Guangzhou incident occurred. Shih had frequent correspondence with them. At that time, the Central Government was focusing all its efforts on suppressing the Communists and had no time to attend to the North, so it had to appease him by increasing his monthly salary. At the same time, Deputy Commander Chang also provided generous assistance, and the situation eased slightly.

▲ The Appointment of Chang Hsueh-cheng: Chang Hsueh-cheng is a graduate of the Japanese Military Academy. He was frustrated in the Northeast. In April, he went to Shunde to persuade Shih to expand his strength, otherwise he would not be able to survive. Shih agreed very much and immediately appointed Chang as the commander of the Third Army and allocated 7,000 to 8,000 surplus rifles. Chang immediately recruited soldiers and issued commissions widely, appointing a total of six division commanders and five mixed brigade commanders. Those who knew the situation knew that this was reckless, but it was very difficult to recruit soldiers in recent years, so he went everywhere to appease bandits and appoint them to official positions. Coal miners in the Lincheng Matouzhen area were mostly forced to become soldiers. The police and militia firearms in the counties under his jurisdiction were all requisitioned. In less than a month, he managed to gather more than 30,000 troops. Shih's military pay became even more insufficient, so he borrowed supplies locally and became increasingly harsh. The county magistrates were unable to raise the funds and resigned one after another, reporting to the province. The Northeast senior generals, seeing Shih acting so recklessly, believed that he must have ambitions, so they secretly prepared. Every sunset, both sides would deploy armed sentries, and the sound of night watchmen would be heard. At dawn, they would withdraw. The situation became tense again.

▲ The Execution of Chang Yun-tse: Shih's Secretary-General, Chang Yun-tse, had been a professor at Jilin University for many years. He was quite talented and deeply trusted by Shih. Seeing that Shih was acting recklessly without considering the pros and cons, he tried to dissuade him slightly, but instead aroused Shih's suspicion. Chang was recommended by a key figure in the Northeast, so he secretly reported Shih's conspiracy to the Northeast. Unexpectedly, the matter was not kept secret and was discovered by Shih. On the night of June 4th, Shih, holding a pistol, sneaked into Chang's bedroom and shot him. He immediately ordered his men to bury him in the wilderness. The rumor that he was buried alive is not true. After Shih killed Chang, he knew that the Northeast could not tolerate him, so he telegraphed to miscellaneous troops and certain generals with historical ties to start an uprising together. The news spread and everyone was alarmed. At that time, Chang Hsueh-liang was ill in the Peking Union Medical College Hospital. His generals were not convenient to ask Chang for instructions on how to deal with the situation, and no one dared to make their own decisions. After several discussions, they decided to urgently dispatch a brigade of artillery and three brigades of infantry into the Shanhaiguan Pass to strengthen defenses and prevent any eventuality. Later, all parties did not think that Shih's appointed date for the uprising was right. Shih felt isolated, so he sent representatives to Beiping to express his obedience to orders and support the Central Government. At this point, the situation had eased on the surface, but was still very tense inside.

▲ Northeast Army Prepares: After Shih's army was reorganized by Chang Hsueh-liang last year, the Central Government designated seven counties bordering Shanxi and Henan as defense areas. Shih was unwilling to leave the railway line, so he remained stationed in Shunde, Shahe, Handan, Cizhou, Cheng'an, Zhangde, and other counties. The general headquarters was located in Shunde, and the training regiment was located in Zhangde. When the Northeast Army entered the Shanhaiguan Pass last year, it sent the 6th Cavalry Brigade, Bai Fengxiang, to station in Shunde, intending to force Shih's army to withdraw from Hebei Province and go to the counties designated by the Central Government to garrison. Shih ignored this. Later, the soldiers of Bai's brigade could not get along with Shih's army, so they withdrew from Shunde and used Neiqiu, Nanhe, Renxian, Yongnian, and other counties as buffer zones, with neither side stationing troops. When suspicions arose, the two sides began to deploy night sentries, and Shih sent troops to station in the buffer zone. When encountering a Northeast Army night patrol company, they would disarm them. Fortunately, the Northeast Army officers all understood the overall situation and avoided conflict, so they reported to their superiors and negotiated with Shih to return the firearms. Shih denied any knowledge of the matter and claimed that nothing had happened. Although the Northeast Army was patient, it was ultimately unhappy. In early this month, Chang Hsueh-liang recovered his health and began to inquire about military and political affairs. He gradually understood the recent actions of Shih's army and felt deeply unhappy. However, in order to maintain peace in North China, he sent representatives to Shandong and Shanxi to declare the intentions of the Central Government to the generals, and mobilized troops to prepare for defense. He also ordered that no matter how Shih's army provoked, our side would never engage in conflict, hoping to prompt Shih to wake up. He also ordered Yu Hsueh-chung to be in charge of the Peiping-Hankou Railway, and Wang Shu-chang to be in charge of the Tianjin-Pukou Railway. It is said that the troop deployment is currently very thorough. (July 18th)

Communist Suppression Army Recovers Shicheng and Jianning 57

▲ Communist Bandits Flee to Ningdu and Ruijin

▲ But Ningdu is Also Under Encirclement

Nanchang Dispatch: After the Communist Suppression Army's left wing captured Guangchang, it went straight to Shicheng and Ningdu, and Jianning in Fujian. On the 16th of this month, Zhu Shaoliang, Zhao Guantao, Chen Cheng, and other troops attacked the Mao bandits from Baishui Town in Guangchang, advancing towards Shicheng. At that time, the Mao bandits believed that this place was related to the contact between the Red bandits in southern Jiangxi and western Fujian, so they personally led 20,000 to 30,000 bandits, including Gu Daogong, Li Wenlin, and Luo Binghui, to resist stubbornly. The Communist Suppression Army took advantage of the victory to drive straight in, and the Red bandits were defeated, suffering heavy casualties. The bandits, seeing that the Communist Suppression Army was irresistible, wanted to win with a surprise attack, flanking and attacking, attempting to bypass Jianning and Ningdu, and encircle the Communist Suppression Army's left and right. The Communist Suppression Army divided its forces to resist, responding calmly, and sent several airplanes to drop heavy bombs on the bandit side, bombing them. The bandits resisted slightly, but were unable to withstand it and fled back to Ningdu and Ruijin. The Communist Suppression Army then recovered Shicheng County. The Headquarters has received an airplane report that there are our army symbols in Baishui, Guangchang, and our army has entered Shicheng. Also, the front-line headquarters yesterday received a telegram from Zhu Commander-in-Chief, that before our army captured Shicheng, Zhu bandits robbed clothes, food, and silver dollars from Fujian, forcing 8,000 to 9,000 farmers to carry loads through Shicheng to Ningdu lair, but our army used lightning speed to capture Shicheng, bandits stolen goods, all were seized by our army. He Yingqin immediately telegraphed Chiang, asking for instructions on how to deal with the 8,000 to 9,000 porters, Chiang specifically ordered to give them money and send them back to their hometowns.

The front-line headquarters recently sent another telegram to Commander-in-Chief Chiang, roughly saying that one unit of our left wing entered Fujian to pursue the bandits, and recovered Jianning on the day before yesterday, capturing more than a thousand Red bandits. Fujian army Liu Heding, Zhang Zhen and other divisions, because the left wing entered Fujian, took a pincer style attack on the Red bandits. The bandits, because Guangchang and Shicheng were lost, Fujian-Jiangxi contact was cut off, extremely panic wanted to break out of the encirclement from Ninghua Changting, was Liu Zhang each division from Yanping Jiangle, severely attacked killed more than a thousand bandits, peasant bandits scattered. Our army has recovered Jianning Shicheng, the vast majority of Red bandits all retreated to Ruijin Ningdu and Xingguo three counties. Also, the camp yesterday received an airplane report, flying to Xingguo Ningdu Donggu and Ruijin area to reconnaissance today, (A) Our right wing has Xingcheng surrounded, cannon sounds rumble, machine guns and rifles sound, dense as continuous cannon, the war is extremely fierce, (B) The left wing to Ningdu for several heavy encirclement, the first line began the general attack, later arrivals endless, bandits with life and death at stake, closed the city stubbornly, our army pounced on the city, planes also to the city bandits dense teams dropped a hundred sixty pounds of bombs four, all have hit explode, killed very many bandits. Heard Chiang with each bandit area successively recovered, yesterday specifically will bandit area forty-three counties of nine nine district chairman announced, order immediately go to each district to work, handle the aftermath, and on the 19th in the camp met with each committee, instructed everything, make effort to work (July 19th)

After Chiang Returns to Nanchang 58

▲ He Jingwu’s Talk to Newspaper Reporters

▲ Chiang's Attitude Toward the Wanbaoshan Incident and Temporary Unwillingness to Return to Nanjing

Nanchang dispatch: After the Wanbaoshan incident occurred, the whole country was indignant. Military reporters and reporters stationed in Jiangxi from Chinese and foreign newspapers visited Chiang at the command center in a group on the 18th, as Chiang had returned to the province from the front line. They asked about the negotiations for the Wanbaoshan incident and the front line's suppression of bandits. Chiang was dealing with central government affairs and reviewing front-line military reports, so he dispatched the Adjutant General of the Headquarters, He Jingwu, to meet them. A transcript of He’s speech is as follows:

▲ Wanbaoshan Incident: Koreans unreasonably shot and killed our country's overseas Chinese, Chairman Chiang was extremely indignant. However, when this happened, Chiang was inspecting the troops on the front line, communication was difficult and the news was delayed. Regarding the details of this matter, it was not very clear. After returning to the provincial capital, he read the records of various newspapers and the detailed report of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and then he knew everything. He immediately sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to protest seriously, argue with reason, in order to achieve the goal of revolutionary diplomacy.

▲ Inspection Trip: After Chiang telegraphed the various armies to begin a general attack, he set off from the province on the 2nd of this month to inspect the troops. On the 3rd and 4th, he arrived at Linchuan (i.e. Fuzhou), stayed for a few days, and then set off for Nancheng and Nanfeng, instructing the various generals on the situation, and inspecting the local party and government facilities, and the suffering of the people. After Chiang arrived at the front line, the morale was boosted, so in less than ten days, Guangchang and Lichuan were recovered. Futian, Tengtian, Zhaoxie, and Kangdu were also occupied one after another. The Red bandits' initial plan was to gather a large number of elite troops (Peng Dehuai and Xiang Ying's 5th and 8th fake armies) in Jianning and Ninghua in western Fujian, to harass our left wing, and attempt to break out of Nanfeng and cut off our army's rear route into Guangchang and Lichuan. Fortunately, our army had prepared early, and concentrated heavy troops in Kangdu, Qianshan, and Shizui, completely resolving Peng's bandits who came from Fujian. At the same time, Guangchang County was captured, and more than 8,000 bandit rifles were seized, and tens of thousands of Red slaves were disbanded. The bandits' plan to harass was completely defeated, and the bandits turned into the people, and many who regretted and came back.

▲ Current Status of the Bandits: The Red bandits have no supplies of food and ammunition, and the bandit soldiers have nothing to eat or wear, and are suffering unspeakably. Peng's bandits have all been resolved in Kangdu, and Zhu's elite troops have also lost almost all of them. Now the bandit remnants have retreated to Ningdu, but Ningdu is mostly plains, and machine guns can be used to sweep them away. It is hoped that they can be wiped out in the shortest possible time.

▲ Chiang Stays in the Province Temporarily: Chiang had made perfect arrangements in the front according to the original plan, so he temporarily returned to Nanchang to reside, and directed everything. He Yingqin is responsible for the military affairs on the front line. Chiang General Commander will not return to Nanjing for the time being, and it has not been decided whether to go to Kuling or not. (July 19th)

The Pyongyang Massacre Report Investigated by the Consulates in Korea 60

The Chinese Consulate General in Korea, the Kuomintang branch in Korea, and the Chinese Chamber of Commerce dispatched personnel to Pyongyang to comfort the Chinese who were in distress and investigate the circumstances of the Korean riot. The entire process has been recorded in previous reports. Now we will further

Chinese Overseas Chinese Who Were Beaten in Seoul 61

Record the full text of the report as follows: We set off for Pyongyang on the evening of the 8th of this month, and arrived at Pyongyang Station the next morning. Immediately, the Japanese governor's office staff Mori Yama and police officer Mori O, and the Dong-A Ilbo reporter Kim Sung-eop surrounded us at the station. A few steps away, there were also sixteen or seventeen representatives of various Korean people's groups. After greeting each other, we walked out of the station. We originally wanted to hire a car to go directly to the Chinese overseas Chinese shelter to comfort the victims and inquire about the details of the victims, but the staff of the governor's office forced us to take the car they had prepared and escorted us to the Pyongyang Hotel. They invited us into an extremely deep room. After exchanging greetings, Mori Yama once again made various alarming threats and shed tears (fake crying) to express his love for the Chinese overseas Chinese. He also told us not to act freely, so as to avoid being attacked by unexpected rioters. After we severely questioned him and said that before we came, we had already asked the chief of the foreign affairs section of the Governor-General's office and the chief of the police department about the truth here. They all said that the place was already peaceful and nothing was happening, so we could go. Therefore, we came here under the orders of our superiors. The mission of this trip is only to comfort the overseas Chinese and inspect the situation of the victims. It has no other purpose. We have already made the determination to sacrifice our lives when we came, and we especially hope that the rioters will quickly attack us to fulfill our benevolence of sacrificing ourselves. In short, no matter what, we must first go to the Chinese overseas Chinese shelter to comfort and inquire. Mori Yama had no reason to answer, so he excused himself to go back to the governor's office to ask the governor for instructions, and then went together.

The Chinese Resident of Seoul who was Beaten 62

After a while, Yanben, the chief secretary of the Pyeongannam-do Governor's Office, came and stated, "It is extremely regrettable that the esteemed residents of your country have suffered this unwarranted disaster. However, post-incident accommodations and other matters have been handled jointly by the provincial and municipal offices, as well as the compassionate relief efforts of the Korean populace. All are now safe and sound." We then stated, "There is no need to discuss the matter of 'giving two jujubes after a slap in the face.' What we want to know is the actual current situation of our compatriots." He said that all 5,200 or so Chinese residents in Pyongyang had been accommodated in the Medical Training Institute and felt very safe. "We (the Japanese) have been working day and night to fulfill our responsibility of protection." We also said, "We have come to express our condolences, not for investigation or negotiation. Please do not say more, and quickly allow us to see our suffering compatriots." He had no choice but to agree, and asked us to wait a moment for permission from his superiors before allowing us to meet. We ordered him to make frequent phone calls. At that time, a reporter from the Dong-A Ilbo came to visit and stated that this unfortunate incident was not the intention of the Korean people, nor was it the work of the Pyongyang Koreans. According to his personal observation, those who committed the violence were all hired from other places by a certain country, specifically to do this. According to his investigation, none of the more than 500 Chinese households were spared; all were destroyed and looted by rioters. 71 men and 12 women were beaten to death with clubs, short knives, etc., for a total of 83 people. 64 men and 9 women were seriously injured, and 33 men and 6 women were slightly injured. All property was lost," and so on. As we were talking, the Japanese man returned from making a phone call, and the reporter hurriedly bid farewell. We then traveled with Japanese police officers in a car to the accommodation center. Along the way, we did not see any signs of alert or instability. Unexpectedly, as the car approached the accommodation center, we saw a large team of Japanese soldiers and police, heavily armed and on high alert, as if facing a major enemy. When the car arrived at the gate, we saw countless compatriots in the courtyard, men, women, old, and young, who had been harmed, with broken heads, swollen legs, broken arms, and blind eyes, which was heartbreaking and unbearable to witness. We were then led by a Japanese gate guard to a room, but we did not see any compatriots. Among those who came to speak with us, we requested to meet with the business association leaders and party comrades among the disaster victims. The Japanese, reluctantly, sent more than ten people, including the business association president Meng Xian Shi, escorted by military police who spoke Chinese. When we met, we stared at each other in silence, unable to say a word. Then, everyone embraced and cried bitterly, unable to make a sound. Later, someone forced out a few words while weeping, saying,

"We have been ordered by Consul General Zhang and the chairman of the business association and the party committee to come and express our condolences, and we are willing to investigate the circumstances of the harm suffered by our compatriots, the true nature of the Korean riot, in order to prepare materials for requesting a serious negotiation with the government." He then advised Chairman Meng to stop crying and report in detail. He said, "Before the incident, I stayed in Andong due to business. I heard rumors of unrest among the Koreans and rushed back to Pyongyang, requesting protection from the Japanese police in Pyongyang. The Japanese police officer said that there was no need to panic and assured us that we would be safe. That night at nine o'clock, a large number of Korean youths started a riot, wielding long sticks, short knives, stones, and bricks. They killed and injured any Chinese they encountered, and destroyed and looted any Chinese households they found. Some blew whistles to give orders, and some shouted slogans to instigate, yelling 'Kill the Hu people.' Hu people is what Koreans call Chinese people. None of the Chinese who encountered them were spared, and not a single Chinese household was left. According to their post-incident investigation, 5,112 people were forcibly detained here by the Japanese police. More than 500 households in the city were destroyed, and more than 500 men, women, old, and young were injured to varying degrees. 216 people were beaten to death, and countless people were missing. Some were even disemboweled and had their hearts gouged out, with livers and intestines scattered everywhere. Even infants in swaddling clothes were not spared, and some had their noses and ears cut off. We have been in Korea for decades, and our property is worth hundreds of thousands, and we have never offended anyone. At the beginning of the riot, some Koreans planned to hide and protect us, but the Japanese police not only did not allow it, but also did not allow us to carry any belongings, only allowing us to be detained here alone, suffering in the open air. Not only could we not move freely, but even news from inside and outside was completely cut off. The riot lasted for two days, with numerous acts of violence, but the Japanese police did not interfere at all. Only after all the Chinese were wiped out did the Japanese military police begin to impose martial law." At this point, the Japanese police did not allow him to continue speaking, and Meng and others burst into tears again, not daring to say more. We then requested the Japanese police to allow all the refugees to meet and receive condolences. The Japanese police excused themselves by saying that the space was limited and they could not gather everyone. We insisted, so they gathered fifty or sixty refugee leaders to talk. Before we could speak, all the representatives burst into tears. We were filled with anger and grief and slapped ourselves in the face several times, expressing that as officials protecting overseas Chinese, we had allowed our compatriots to suffer so much and could not fulfill our duties, feeling ashamed and unable to face anyone. We asked our compatriots to especially forgive our helplessness due to the lack of any police power. We then told the disaster-stricken compatriots several points: (1) The tragedy suffered by our compatriots this time is beyond the expectations of any civilized country in the world. In this so-called civilized and law-abiding country under Japanese rule, such a major massacre and act of violence has occurred. I don't know where the Japanese police have gone. Therefore, regarding this planned massacre, we will not ask the people of the subjugated Korea, but we will seriously negotiate with the Japanese state. (2) Our Eastern spirit has always valued universal love and the principle of great unity. This tragedy has even killed many ignorant infants, which is truly a bankruptcy of Eastern morality to the extreme. We are not only ashamed for the Korean people and for the Japanese officials and civilians ruling Korea, but also feel unfortunate for the Chinese people, the center of our Eastern civilization. (3) Regarding this tragedy, we do not have to hate the great Japanese Empire, but we should thank the lessons of the great Japanese Empire. Our weakness and strength, the theory of self-strengthening with might but without justice, our great sacrifice this time can be considered the price of awakening. Now that things have come to this, I hope you will not think of fighting with your bare hands. Since there was no resistance before, we can only let the Japanese kill or spare us as they please, and wait for the sympathy, assistance, and negotiation of the government of our country, the Chinese Kuomintang, the Chinese business associations, and the civilized countries of the world."

While someone was speaking, the Japanese police forcibly stopped him three times, but we thought that since things had come to this, it was still not allowed for officials of our country to say a few words of self-blame, which was truly unreasonable. Therefore, we did not listen to the prohibition. After someone finished speaking, Comrade Zheng intended to express his opinion as a representative of the Chinese Kuomintang, but the Japanese police ultimately did not allow it. We then went to various places to inspect and saw thousands of female compatriots, holding more than 300 babies, crying together, swarming towards us, pulling at us, and shouting for help. We were empty-handed, and our hearts were filled with fear and sorrow, and we cried together, shedding tears of sympathy. When the Japanese military police saw this scene, they feared a major incident, so they carried out an emergency mobilization, preparing to fire, surrounding us, and not allowing us to cry anymore, even hitting women and children with rifle butts, not allowing them to cry anymore. Fortunately, a certain gentleman was alert and secretly took several photos of the tragic situation amidst the noisy voices, which could be used as a reference for future negotiations. The most tragic thing was that not only were ordinary farmers and workers greatly abused, but even the business association president and other leaders had to sleep on damp ground in grass sheds and eat sticky rice balls. The wealth accumulated through more than 20 years of blood and sweat was lost in an instant, and they still had to endure such great suffering. What was even more unbearable was that they had to represent the disaster-stricken compatriots and thank the Japanese side. As we were urgently inspecting, an official from the provincial office suddenly came to invite us to the provincial office to talk, otherwise we would not be able to inspect freely. We had no choice but to go to the provincial office. When we got in the car, one of the business association leaders tried to go with us to see the provincial governor, but he was pulled back by the Japanese police. When we arrived at the provincial office, we saw that the Japanese all looked panicked, but pretended to be calm. When we saw the provincial governor, the chief of internal affairs, and the chief of police, we were filled with anger and did not know what to say. They expressed their gratitude to us, and we replied that we were busy. Later, the chief of internal affairs asked us in a stern tone why we had stirred up the excitement of the refugees. We then loudly told him that the refugees were in a foreign country and were brutally murdered by foreigners for no reason. When they saw officials from their own country, it was like seeing their parents. How could they not cry and express their grievances? As for us, we uphold public justice and fairness, and your country does not need to ask too much to avoid creating more bad feelings. They then softened their tone and boasted about their efforts to protect the overseas Chinese, and showed us the provincial office's notice. However, it was nothing more than a proclamation inciting Koreans to massacre Chinese. Before we finished talking, the provincial governor had already secretly ordered someone to prepare a Western meal. When we saw that the table had been set, we forcibly bid farewell, telling them that our compatriots were suffering in the accommodation center and that we had come to express our condolences, so how could we enjoy ourselves here? We were also afraid that your government office would be suspected of bribery, which would be even worse. They did not dare to keep us any longer. After we left, we were surrounded by Japanese newspaper reporters who asked us what our impressions were of this trip. We replied, "Only one word: barbaric behavior." They then insisted on taking a photo of us, and we asked the Japanese police to take us to the cemetery in the jurisdiction of the Daidong Police Station in the suburbs to pay our respects to the overseas Chinese who had been killed. The Japanese police were reluctant, but after we repeatedly requested, they agreed to first take us to the Pyongyang Hospital and then to the cemetery. We first went to the hospital and saw more than 200 seriously injured overseas Chinese men and women, and 30 or 40 children, all with serious head injuries, who were unlikely to survive. As we were inspecting, two people died before our eyes, and the tragic situation was beyond words. After leaving the hospital, we took a car to the cemetery. Unexpectedly, the car deliberately went the wrong way, detouring for more than 20 miles, and we saw that the vegetable gardens of the overseas Chinese had all been looted and their huts had been burned down. The most convincing evidence of the Japanese conspiracy was that next to the Daidong County Office and west of the Daidong Police Headquarters, the large Chinese flour mill and soy sauce garden were also burned and looted. We don't know how the Japanese authorities can explain this. After several hours, we finally arrived at the cemetery, where we saw dozens of Japanese police officers helping Korean workers hurriedly bury the dead bodies. When they saw us, they pretended to be compassionate and said that the Korean rioters were too hateful and that the people they killed were too pitiful. Fortunately, the Japanese authorities chose this place to bury them and hired workers to repair the graves. We asked how many people had already been buried, and they replied, "Not many, not many, only a little over 90 people." We then asked how many children had been killed, and they replied, "Only five or six." Alas, according to the Japanese report, there were already so many, let alone the actual number. I remember that during the Gengzi Incident (Boxer Rebellion), the Chinese only killed one Japanese clerk, which led to the invasion of the Eight-Nation Alliance and a great disaster for our country. But now, the massacre is so huge, yet no country has come out to speak up for justice. The so-called grave repair by the Japanese was just burying five or six communal mounds of flesh. We bowed four times to the graves, cried a few times, and Comrade Zheng delivered two sentences. A certain comrade took photos to commemorate it. We returned to the city and inspected the Chinese Chamber of Commerce. Not only was the entire Chamber of Commerce destroyed and smashed by the rioters, but the national flag and consular passports were also torn into pieces. The portrait of the founder Sun Yat-sen was trampled into scrap paper, the party flag was stained with blood, and the party plaque was split into two pieces, because the party headquarters was attached to the Chamber of Commerce. We took

Page 11

Important News

photos, and the Japanese police even threatened us with another attack by Korean rioters. What could be more ridiculous? We are willing to die, so what is the point of scaring us? We finally took photos and left, then took a car back to Seoul to report. Regarding the results of this inspection, we conclude that this major massacre was entirely under Japanese rule and was carried out in a planned manner. Its cruelty is unprecedented, a hundred times more barbaric than the remnants of Baluchi's group in Nikolaevsk. Is this how civilized countries act? Is this how friendship and love are proclaimed? Thinking of this makes one shudder. May all the people of our country be aware of this, and may all the people of the world be aware of this. (Among the 5,200 refugees detained, there were 900 women and children who were too terrified. The refugees asked the Japanese police to allow them to return to their country to reassure them, but the Japanese police did not allow it. This is recounted here.) (July 10)

Attitude of Korean Residents in Jilin Toward China 63

▲Issuing a Declaration 丨 Expressing Goodwill

▲Kim Ri-sam 丨 Was Assassinated

Jilin dispatch: The attitude of Korean residents in Jilin toward the Sino-Korean incident is highly noteworthy. Our authorities are both earnestly advising them and strictly guarding against them. As a result, the 600,000 Korean residents have not taken any unusual actions. They have also organized a committee to investigate the Wanbaoshan Incident, thoroughly investigating and understanding that our side has not oppressed the Korean residents in any way. The massacre of Chinese in the Korean territory was due to being misled, which damaged the goodwill between the Chinese and Korean nations. In addition to sending a telegram to Gyeongseong to convey to all the Korean people to recognize the facts and not to riot again, they also issued a declaration to China expressing their regret. The original text is as follows:

A respectful message to all Chinese compatriots: The Wanbaoshan Incident was originally a very minor issue, but because the Japanese police in Changchun mobilized their forces and Japan incited anti-Chinese sentiment in Korea, it has surprisingly become a major issue in Sino-Japanese negotiations and Sino-Korean relations. As this issue escalates and rumors abound, we feel it is necessary and obligatory to issue a solemn declaration. Since Korea was ravaged by the Japanese railway, our people and passionate youth have been planning independence every day. During this period, due to our historical and geographical ties with China, we have received considerable assistance from our Chinese compatriots. No one with a brain and knowledge does not appreciate China's magnanimous attitude. Under these circumstances, we should show extreme goodwill to our Chinese compatriots so that we do not betray them. However, human nature is uneven, and it is difficult to distinguish between good and bad, so the unfortunate events of the Wanbaoshan Incident and the anti-Chinese sentiment in Korea occurred, which truly fills us with remorse, hatred, and sadness. Although these two incidents were instigated and manipulated by the Japanese, we cannot help but feel regret and shame. We have thoroughly investigated the Wanbaoshan Incident and confirmed that it was the work of pro-Japanese running dogs (Kim Dong-man, Lee Hong-ju, Lee Deok-seo, Lee Jo-hwa, etc.). These people are the greatest public enemies of our Korean independence movement and deserve to be killed. Now, Japan is using them to create antagonism between China and Korea and to disrupt China's security, which is even more unforgivable. Japan is also using this opportunity to play tricks in Korea, creating false rumors and inciting Koreans to commit violence against Chinese residents. The Japanese police not only did not stop them, but secretly sent some Japanese, disguised in civilian clothes, to join the crowd and commit barbaric acts of destroying Chinese businesses and harming Chinese residents, making the Chinese adopt the same narrow-minded attitude as Japan. If this continues, the Korean people living in the three northeastern provinces will have no place to live. In addition to our heartache, we would like to make the following statements: On the one hand, we will advise the Koreans under the command of the Japanese imperialists to repent and quickly leave Wanbaoshan. If they do not, we will definitely use the final means against these hateful elements. On the other hand, we have already informed our compatriots at home about the Wanbaoshan Incident, so that they know that Chinese officials and people have not harmed the Korean farmers in any way. Do not be used by the Japanese, quickly stop the violence, and restore goodwill to the Chinese residents. The facts have already been reported in the newspapers, and Chinese compatriots may have already read them. How should China and Korea work together to defeat this evil Japanese invasion of Manchuria and Mongolia? The shortcut is to first eliminate the shameless running dogs, and then find ways to fight against the imperialists. The Japanese have now organized the "Great Alliance of Japanese Autonomy in Manchuria" to plan for the invasion by the people. At this time, we should unite the Chinese and Korean nations, organize popular organizations, and use the solidarity of the people to confront them and eliminate their invasion as the most important way. We should also awaken the ignorant peasant masses from the temptation of imperialism and provide them with ideological and political training so as to avoid future troubles. In short, the happiness and friendship of our Chinese and Korean nations cannot be achieved until the Japanese imperialists are defeated. We must not be deceived by the Japanese imperialist conspiracy, and we must fight together to achieve our goal. With this, we swear to our beloved 400 million Chinese compatriots. Our slogans are: 1. Oppose Japanese interference in the Wanbaoshan Incident; 2. The Korean farmers in Wanbaoshan must leave immediately; 3. The Chinese and Korean nations unite; 4. Down with pro-Japanese running dogs; 5. Down with Japanese imperialism. Jilin Korean Overseas Wanbaoshan Incident Investigation Committee.

Kim Ri-sam, a reporter from a Korean newspaper stationed in Changchun, previously made provocative propaganda between the Chinese and Korean nations in Korean newspapers regarding the case of Korean farmers forcibly cultivating terraced fields in Wanbaoshan. This led to the massacre of Chinese residents by Koreans in various places in Korea. Recently, Kim, due to criticism from his own Korean people, specially came to Jilin to apologize to various Chinese parties, and submitted articles to various Chinese newspapers clearly stating that he had been deceived and had made mistakes that were unfavorable to Sino-Korean propaganda. The Japanese side, seeing his change of attitude, dispatched Korean police officer Park Chang-ha and several other Koreans from the consulate to Kim's residence at the Far East Hotel, which was set up by Koreans in the commercial port, at 12:00 noon on the 15th. They shot Kim seven or eight times, killing him instantly, and injuring a Chinese passerby named Li En.

Ting Yiming, a policeman from our bureau, rushed to the scene after hearing the gunshots and captured the murderer on the spot and took him to the bureau for investigation. (July 15)

Kong Hechong's Bandit Troops Fled into Southern Hubei 64

▲The Bandit Troops were Defeated by Guo's Troops

Hankou dispatch: About 4,000 remnants of the Red Bandit Kong Hechong recently fled into Mushigang, Yangxin County, Hubei Province, and their momentum was very rampant. Guo Rudong's troops stationed in the area suppressed them. Guo also transferred the regiments stationed in Daye and concentrated them to suppress the bandits in Baishapu. By the morning of the 20th, the bandits were defeated. Kong himself led his troops to flee to the Sanxikou area, more than 60 miles south of Yangxin, and their situation was extremely embarrassing. After Guo won this victory, he reorganized his troops to pursue and suppress them, and telegraphed the Wuhan headquarters, requesting that the troops stationed in the neighboring areas act in unison. It is said that the headquarters has sent an airplane and a warship to patrol the Daye, Yangxin, and Huanggang areas, and the airplane is responsible for covering and dropping bombs. It is expected that the bandits can be completely eliminated in a few days. Near the Tongcheng County area, more than 1,000 Red Bandits have also fled from the Hunan border and are looting in the Shuibeilong area. Xie Bin's troops stationed in the area have sent teams to defeat the bandits and are pursuing them toward Xingjing. (July 20)

He Chengjun Goes to Jiangxi to Meet Chiang 65

▲Xia Douyin and Others Accompany Him

Hankou dispatch: He Chengjun, the director of the Wuhan headquarters, had previously planned to go to Nanchang to meet Generalissimo Chiang, report on the military and political situation in Hubei Province, the recent progress in bandit suppression, and request instructions on everything. However, Chiang Generalissimo moved to Fuzhou, so he did not make the trip. Recently, Chiang has returned to Nanchang and telegraphed He to go to meet him. He then took the Yihua Company's Ruihe wheel eastward to Xun on the night of the 19th, accompanied by Xia Douyin, commander of the Wuhan Garrison, Liu Hangchen, director of the Finance Department of the Sichuan Provincial Rehabilitation Supervision Office, and others, to transfer to Nanchang. Those who came to the ship to see him off included Xu Yuanquan, Zhu Chuanjing, Chen Guangzu, etc. After He left, Chen Guangzu and Zhu Chuanjing jointly handled the affairs of the headquarters. The chairman of the provincial government meeting was temporarily replaced by Liu Wendao, director of the Department of Civil Affairs, and routine official duties were performed by Peng Jieshi, the secretary-general. It is said that He will go to Jiangxi for about four or five days and then return to Hankou. His important tasks, in addition to reporting on the progress of bandit suppression, are probably also to request instructions on the political situation in the north. (July 20)

The 31st State Council Meeting of the Executive Yuan 66

▲Resolved to Appoint Xu Shiying and Others as Members of the Relief Committee

The Executive Yuan held its 31st State Council meeting on the 21st. The attendees were Song Ziwen, Li Shuhua, Ma Fuxiang, Wang Zhengting, Wang Boqun, and Lian Shenghai. Zheng Hongnian, Zhang Wohua, Chen Shaokuan, and Chen Yi attended as observers. Song Ziwen chaired the meeting. (A) Matters for reporting: (1) Minister Wang of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs reported on the progress of negotiations on the anti-Chinese case of the Korean riots and requested that it be reviewed and recorded. (2) Minister Yang of the Ministry of Navy sent a telegram reporting on the return to Fujian to supervise the division and that the naval affairs should be handled by Vice Minister Chen Shaokuan during the period of bandit suppression in Fujian. (3) The Ministry of Railways submitted a proposal for the completion of the Yuehan Railway, proposing to carry out construction in sections at both the north and south ends simultaneously in order to achieve success as soon as possible. Please indicate whether to approve. (4) The ministries, commissions, provincial governments, and municipal governments submitted a total of 14 administrative plans and work reports. (B) Matters for discussion: (1) The Ministry of Navy submitted the amended regulations on naval uniforms and requested that they be reviewed and submitted to the National Government for implementation. Resolution: Submit to the National Government for promulgation. (2) The Anti-Opium Committee submitted the amended rules for awarding anti-opium fines and requested that they be reviewed and implemented. Resolution: Approved and submitted to the National Government for record, and ordered the Anti-Opium Committee to amend and promulgate them. (3) The Board of Trustees for the Management of the British Boxer Indemnity submitted the regulations of the Committee for the Purchase of Materials with the British Returned Boxer Indemnity and requested that they be reviewed and recorded. Resolution: Amended and approved. (4) Resolution: Please appoint Wang Fangting as the Director of the Department of Industry of the Shandong Provincial Government. (5) Resolution: Approve the request of Sun Hegao, Counselor of the Ministry of Railways, to resign. Appointment of Zhu Lvyun to succeed him in the vacant position. (6) Resolution: In addition to the ex officio members of the Relief Committee, please reappoint Xu Shiying, Wang Zhen, Liu Zhenhua, Wang Shouzhen, Zhu Qinglan, Xiong Xiling, Yan Zhuang, Shui Zi, Li Huanying, and Li Jin as members, and appoint Xu Shiying as the Chairman of the Committee, and Wang Zhen, Liu Zhenhua, Wang Shouzhen, and Zhu Qinglan as Standing Committee members.

Photograph of Wu Yabei After Being Assassinated. Wu Yabei, Leader of the Jiujiang Labor Union, Was Assassinated. Wu Yabei, leader of the Jiujiang Labor Union, was elected as a representative to the National Assembly this time and went to Beijing to attend the meeting. After the meeting, he returned to Xun, but unexpectedly, he was suddenly assassinated at 12:00 midnight on the 14th of this month. He had a total of 21 wounds all over his body, and his death was very tragic. 67

Hankou Court Bribery Case Closed 69

▲ Defendant Xu Xuehai and others given non-prosecution disposition

The case of Gao Wei vs. Gao Jiazhi in Hankou, involving a property dispute and allegations of collusion and bribery between lawyers and judges, caused a media uproar. The Hankou Lawyers Association reported the matter, and the Supreme Court transferred the investigation to the Jiujiang District Court. Now, the prosecutor of that court, in addition to separately prosecuting lawyer Teng Wensui and Chief Prosecutor Wang Qing, has decided not to prosecute the handling prosecutor Wang Jue, Xu Xuehai, and related person Wang Huazhen due to insufficient evidence of criminal suspicion. The disposition order is recorded below:

Defendant Xu Xuehai, Wang Jue, Wang Huazhen, the defendants listed on the right are suspected of fraud and dereliction of duty. After investigation, it is deemed that they should not be prosecuted. The factual and legal reasons are stated below: Gao Jiazhi, a wealthy merchant in Hankou, was involved in a property dispute with Gao Wei. Gao Wei entrusted lawyer Teng Wensui to handle the case. Fearing failure, she also initiated criminal proceedings for forgery and embezzlement. While under investigation, she further accused Gao Jiazhi of smoking opium. He was examined at the municipal hospital and detention center. Gao Jiazhi, exhausted by the repeated lawsuits, sought reconciliation with Gao Wei, offering 3,000 yuan in cash and five houses. Gao Wei, knowing her claims were unreasonable, agreed to settle. At that time, rumors spread, causing much discussion. The Hankou Lawyers Association received a confidential letter alleging collusion and bribery between lawyers and judges. The Wuchang Higher Procuratorate also received this letter and summoned the handling personnel Wang Jue, Xu Xuehai, and Chief Prosecutor Wang Qing for questioning about the actual situation. Separate records were made and submitted for transfer of jurisdiction. The Supreme Court ruled that the first instance of this case should be managed by this court. After repeated hearings and investigations, although there were multiple defendants, the existence of facts and evidence should be determined separately. In addition to separately prosecuting Teng Wensui and others, the reasons for those with insufficient suspicion are explained separately: (1) Wang Jue was handling the criminal case of Gao Wei. After the settlement, a relative from Jinan Town held Yu Liangcheng's name card, asking if this person had lobbied the court. Wang Jue was surprised and, considering he had not committed any illegal acts, initiated investigative procedures upon hearing of the official fraud allegations, immediately arresting Yu Liangcheng and questioning lawyer Teng to get to the bottom of the matter and fulfill his duties. However, Chief Prosecutor Wang Qing suggested leniency and repeatedly urged for Yu Liangcheng to be released on bail, which Wang Jue consistently refused. Unable to persist, he transferred the case to another officer and refused to accept illegal orders. With no evidence of criminal acts, there was no suspicion of dereliction of duty. (2) Xu Xuehai took over the Yu Liangcheng fraud case on the morning of November 15th. Wang Jue did not inform him of Wang Qing's suggestion, so he was unaware of the content. On the same day, Wang Qing ordered Xu Xuehai to release Yu Liangcheng on bail. Xu reviewed the case file and, finding no reason to disobey, released Yu Liangcheng on bail with a guarantee from Sanjia Dian to show his seriousness. "See record of this office on June 22nd." After the bail, Wang Qing said that Yu Liangcheng was a person who gets things done and should be dealt with quickly. Xu did not comply and soon left the court due to other matters, with no criminal suspicion to support the allegations. (3) Jiang Huazhen is Chief Wang Qing's cousin. Outsiders used her name to spread rumors about litigation, causing much discussion, but Wang Huazhen was unaware of this. This office is conducting a thorough investigation. Wang Qing presented a letter from Wang Huazhen interceding for Yu Liangcheng, but the letter was not stamped, and the handwriting did not match. Furthermore, the fake letter was mailed from the Hankou Post Office on November 13th of the previous year, as evidenced by the postmark. According to Wang Huazhen, she was in Nanjing in mid-November, helping her husband stamp and collect funds from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, presenting the receipt for proof. "The photo of the receipt is dated November 11th and attached to the file." This shows she was not in Hankou at the time, which is credible. Upon reviewing the forged letter, which used Wang Huazhen's name to intercede for Yu Liangcheng, and observing the defendant, she was confirmed to have no shared fraudulent intent and should not be discussed further. In conclusion, the criminal suspicion of defendants Wang Jue, Xu Xuehai, and Wang Huazhen is deemed insufficient. In accordance with Article 244, Section 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law, a decision not to prosecute is hereby issued as right. Prosecutor Xiong Li, June 29th

Local Correspondence

Suzhou 70

Torrential Rains Cause Disaster, Villagers Report Famine: Continuous torrential rains in Suzhou recently have caused rivers to rise sharply. Low-lying areas in various townships have become watery regions. Villagers in places like Chefang, the East Mountain, and the West Mountain have already submitted petitions to the county government and the finance bureau in the past few days, reporting the disaster and requesting that officials be dispatched to the villages to survey the situation. The government and bureau have instructed them to make every effort to pump out the accumulated water in order to save the crops. However, the torrential rains have not stopped immediately, and only the early rice has been damaged. If the weather does not clear up soon, the late rice will also be unsalvageable.

Rape of a Young Girl, Appeal Judgment: Liao Yonghua, a 63-year-old stonemason from Wuxi, was sentenced to seven years in prison by Wuxi County for raping a seven-year-old girl, Cai Su'e. Liao appealed to the High Court, which issued a judgment on the 20th, reducing the sentence to four years in prison.

New Finance Bureau Chief to Take Office Tomorrow: Yuan Xiaogu, the chief of the Wuxian County Finance Bureau, has been approved to resign. Shen Bingzhan, the chief of the Songjiang County Finance Bureau, has been transferred to succeed him. Shen has already sent personnel to Suzhou to make arrangements and is scheduled to take office on the 23rd. Shen himself may arrive in Suzhou last night or this morning. Yuan's predecessor has completed the handover procedures and is preparing to transfer the office.

Wuxi 71

Representatives of Fresh Meat Businesses from Various Counties Go to Beijing and the Province to Petition: Since the government implemented the elimination of "li" tax and the adoption of a business tax for the fresh meat industry throughout Jiangsu Province, petitions have been repeatedly submitted to the Ministry of Finance requesting the abolition of the original slaughter tax and the adoption of the business tax, and also requesting a clear date for the abolition. However, approval has not yet been granted. The industry associations from various counties recently sent representatives to Wuxi to gather and discuss the matter. It was decided that the representatives would go to the provincial capital to petition. Representatives from Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Taixing, Shanghai, Kunshan, Wujin, Wuxi, Yizheng, Danyang and other counties were designated as representatives to petition the ministry and the province. They were requesting that, in accordance with the supplementary measures to the outline established by the ministry, after the implementation of the business tax law, the provisions for merging or abolishing the previous slaughter tax be implemented. At the same time, they will also go to the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office in Nanjing to petition, in order to achieve their goals.

Two Robbery Cases Cracked, Stolen Goods Recovered: Xue Furui, the captain of the detective team of the County Public Security Bureau, received a tip-off a few days ago stating that multiple robbers involved in the robbery of the chief of Lengdu Township's house and the farmer Zhang Boguan's house in Houyangfang Qianqingshiqiao were hiding near the city. Captain Xue, upon receiving the report, immediately gathered all the detectives and arrested the suspects. He first arrested Hu Shijin and Gu A'er, both from Tongzhou, and recovered many stolen goods in Zhoushanbang. They confessed that there were still fugitives in the workshops outside the East Gate and under the Baqiao Bridge outside the West Gate. Captain Xue immediately dispatched officers to search separately. Xu Dexin was arrested in the workshop outside the East Gate, and Zhang Xianda was arrested in the Hongfuyuan teahouse outside the West Gate. All were sent to the County Public Security Bureau for interrogation. The robbers all confessed to robbing the Miao and Zhang families and distributing the stolen goods. They were ordered to be detained pending transfer to the County Court for interrogation.

Changshu 72

Battalion Commander Clash with Finance Bureau Chief Over Disbursement: The expenses of the Jiangsu Provincial Pacification and Security Force are assigned to this county, which is responsible for 5,000 yuan per month. The Jiangci Group sends personnel to Changshu to collect the funds on a monthly basis. Since the arrival of the Second Battalion of the First Regiment to reside in our county, the head of the Zhu Chumin militia has obtained approval from the Security Office to directly allocate the 5,000 yuan that the county's Finance Bureau is responsible for to the Second Battalion as military pay. Previously, when Head Zhu came to Changshu on orders to investigate the Hupu bandit case, he had discussed the matter with Zhuang Yeguang, the head of the county's Finance Bureau, urging him to quickly allocate 2,000 yuan for food expenses. It was agreed to pay in two installments. The 18th was the date for the first payment. Shen Yiming, the battalion commander of the Second Battalion of the garrison, took the payment voucher from the regimental headquarters to the Finance Bureau and met with Bureau Chief Zhuang Yeguang. To his surprise, Zhuang did not honor the agreement regarding the military expenses, claiming that there were no funds available at the time. Battalion Commander Shen said that the expenses were for the soldiers' food and could not be delayed. Moreover, it was a previously agreed date. If the food supply was cut off, who would be responsible? At that time, the head of the Finance Bureau continued to prevaricate and even retorted. As a result, Battalion Commander Shen became furious and severely reprimanded him. (It is said that he slapped Zhuang twice.) Subsequently, Shen and Zhuang went to the county government to report everything to the county magistrate. Fortunately, Magistrate Tan did his best to mediate and promised to allocate 800 yuan in silver to meet the urgent need by the 20th of this month. The matter was then settled.

Jiangyin 73

Li Leng Case, Non-Prosecution Disposition: The former county magistrate, Li Leng, was investigated by Shi Zechen, dispatched by the High Court, for an opium bribery case. He was handed over to the Wuxian District Court for interrogation. This had been done three times. On the 19th, according to news from Suzhou, the local procuratorate issued a non-prosecution disposition for the Li Leng case.

A Corpse Case Turns into a Farce: The red boat of the North Wai Yidu Bureau salvaged an unidentified female corpse from the river a few days ago. At that time, Hong, the concubine of Shen Huaigui, the owner of the Dayichun store, had been missing for several days. People such as Zhu Jinru suspected that the female corpse was Shen's concubine, so Huaigui went to identify the body. The face of the female corpse had already decomposed. Because the clothes and shape were not right, he did not recognize her. Subsequently, the county government sent an examining officer to verify the body. The Shen family also sent people to Shizhuang, Rugao, to the home of Hong's mother to inquire about news. To their surprise, Hong and her four-year-old daughter were safely at home. Because the main wife did not tolerate her, she had not returned home. After reporting back to Cheng, the doubts of the public were difficult to resolve. Even Magistrate Peng did not fully believe it. On the 19th, he summoned Shen Huaigui, ordering him to hand over Hong within three days. The reporter also found this matter strange and personally visited Shizhuang a few days ago to investigate. He indeed saw Hong and her daughter safely at home. However, a corpse case has already caused a sensation throughout the city.

Danyang 74

Robbers in the Northeast Township Rob and Injure People: The home of Pan Xiaoyu, a farmer in Panjia Village, Henan, Lingkou, in the Eastern Township, was suddenly broken into at 11 p.m. last night by several robbers speaking in mixed dialects and wielding guns. They extensively searched the house, twisted Xiaoyu, and forced him to hand over cash, burning him with fire. When nearby villagers sounded gongs and shouted for help, the robbers scattered and fled. The home of Mo Jinsheng in Mojia Village in the Northern Township was also broken into by several robbers who forced their way inside and searched the house. Jinsheng was severely burned with fire and may not survive. The case has now been reported and police have been asked to apprehend the robbers.

Robbers Posing as Transport Personnel Arrested: The home of Wu Yaogui in Dengjia Village in the Eastern Township was robbed some days ago, suffering heavy losses. Sima Shusheng, a key criminal in the case, suddenly joined the conscription office of the garrison police stationed in Danyang as a transport personnel in order to avoid being noticed after receiving his share of the stolen goods. This was discovered by the county's detective team, which reported the information to the County Public Security Bureau, who prepared a document and sent personnel to the garrison police to bring Sima Shusheng in for interrogation.

Multiple Drownings at Dengjia Bridge: Due to continuous heavy rain in recent days, the river at Dengjia Bridge in the Eastern Township has risen sharply. The wooden structure of the bridge has been washed away by the water. The local people, in order to facilitate transportation, have set up a wooden raft to provide passage. Unexpectedly, yesterday morning, seven male and female passengers boarded the raft and started towards the center of the river. The stern of the boat suddenly leaked, causing panic among the passengers, which led to the wooden raft falling apart. All fell into the water. Only Ding Shigeng, a blind man, managed to climb ashore and escape. The rest drowned. It was truly tragic.

Nantong 75

Finance and Agriculture Bureaus Thoroughly Investigate Hemp Gum Tax: The Finance and Agriculture and Mining Bureaus have repeatedly received petitions from coastal fishermen in the Jiangbei, Tong, and Ru counties, accusing Liu Xiaoshu and others of illegally collecting hemp gum tax, with annual revenues of more than 2,000 yuan. This tax was originally required for the green camp troops stationed along the coast during the Qing Dynasty's Kangxi era, with hemp used by soldiers to weave shoes and glue used for arrows. It has continued to this day without being abolished. The Finance Bureau has dispatched Inspector Yuan Chengzen, and the Agriculture and Mining Bureau has appointed Shen Susheng to come to Tong and then go to Juegang and Fengli to thoroughly investigate the matter.

Disputes Over Converting Copper Coins into Silver Dollars: The public funds for education and charity in Tongyi have always been deposited in money shops for interest. In the past, everything was calculated in copper coins. In recent years, disputes have arisen over the conversion to copper dollars. The county government has specially petitioned the High Court for resolution.

Yu Shenshou Case, Complaint Withdrawn: After Yu Jue and Zhang Xiaoruo reached a settlement in the Yu Shenshou case, the civil court of the Nantong County Court has approved Yu Jue's withdrawal of the complaint against Zhang. The Nantong County Government also reported the situation to the provincial government on the 20th to close the case. However, the tomb of Ms. Yu Shenshou is located under Huangni Mountain. Currently, the riverbank is collapsing severely, and the tomb is getting closer to the river, making it difficult to avoid being washed away.

Zhenjiang 76

Trial Involves Suspicions of Bribery: Gaogang in Jingjiang County has always been an area rife with smuggling. A large amount of opium was discovered there a month ago. The military police investigated the case, and the involved parties abandoned the opium in the river. Wei Sanguan recovered it and was arrested by the county government. The judgment was hasty and involved suspicions of bribery. The matter was learned by Liu Zhenzhi, a local, who filed a complaint with the High Court, stating that County Magistrate Wang Jiwu and Public Security Bureau Chief Jin Ming'an were suspected of shielding the guilty. After receiving the complaint, Dean Lin secretly ordered a thorough investigation. Finding that there was cause for the investigation, he sent the case to the Zhenjiang Court for interrogation. After receiving the order, the court studied the case and issued 15 summons yesterday, scheduling a hearing for 8 a.m. on the 24th to investigate. Those summoned were Wang Jiwu, the County Magistrate of Jingjiang, and Liang Wei, Huang Weibang, Yao Zhusan, Xu Ming'en, Chen Chao, Lu Zhuoqun, Wang Jiadian, Lu Haoran, Liu Zancheng, Zhu Boyu, Du Zhihe, Zhu Zhongyi, Wan Tianyi, who handled the case, and the plaintiff Liu Zhenzhi.

Yangzhou 77

Flood Victims Flock South: The recent rainfall in Jiangbei has been heavy, and the river and lake waters have been high, far exceeding those of the Republic of China's tenth year, making the dikes along the more than 400-li Grand Canal precarious. It has been heard that the section of the dike at Jieshou on the border of Gaobao has collapsed beyond repair. The town has been gathering more than 2,000 people for the past few days to protect the dike. As a result, the Yangzhou public's fear of cars has led to the suspension of bus services yesterday. The rural normal school buildings in the town are also in danger. Yesterday and today, boats of flood victims flowing down the river have been continuously arriving along the Guayang area. However, Yangzhou is still experiencing heavy rain today, causing great concern among the citizens.

Qingjiang 78

The Battle Between Soldiers and Bandits at Yugou: Due to local bandits demanding an exorbitant sum of 20,000 yuan in taxes in Yugou Town, Huaiyin Fourth District, all the merchants and residents of the town fled. On the 14th of this month, more than 100 representatives, including Wu Qiqing, Luo Zhaolun, Gao Zixi, and Zheng Heting, came to the city to petition. Liang, the commander of the 25th Route, sent Battalion Commander Kong of the First Regiment of the Independent Brigade with two squads of soldiers to defend and suppress the bandits on the 15th. They arrived at 11 a.m. today. At that time, the town's militia and bandits were engaged in a firefight at Zhuzhuang to the east of Langshi. Battalion Commander Kong immediately led his troops there. Unexpectedly, the bandits occupied the houses and fired out, showing no fear. Kong ordered his troops to throw a hand grenade, setting the houses on fire. The bandits then fled outward. As a result, one member of the defense force was killed, and two soldiers of Battalion Commander Kong were wounded. Two bandits were killed, and two bandits were captured alive. In the afternoon at 7 p.m., the government troops returned to the Yugou Fortress to rest. On the morning of the 16th, Battalion Commander Kong was ordered to return to Yangzhuang for inspection. However, the people of Yugou were still uneasy. Therefore, yesterday (the 16th) morning, more than 400 people came to the city to petition again.

Huzhou 82

Bandits Rob Silk Boat in Broad Daylight: At around 3 p.m. today (the 20th), in the Yangjiazhuang area, about seven li outside the West Gate of this city, a silk-selling boat from Hongxingqiao to Huzhou was stopped by two bandits wearing blue cloth clothes and holding wooden-cased guns. The boat owner, Qian Yinshou, and more than a dozen passengers were carrying more than a dozen carts of silk. Upon seeing the two bandits standing on the East Bridge, they ordered the silk boat to stop. The boat owner saw that the bandits had weapons and had to dock. After the bandits boarded the boat, they forced the boat to dock in a small harbor, arbitrarily searching the passengers and robbing them of more than 20 yuan in silver. The bandits were still not satisfied and wanted to take the silk. After repeated pleas from the passengers, the bandits took three carts of silk, went ashore, and left.

A period of three months has been set, stipulating that at least 30% of the old taxes should be collected each month to meet the deadline.

In accordance with the old custom of this county, half of the rent is divided equally, and 25% is deducted as the standard for revising the new lease. Hangzhou 85

Military Training Center to Begin Training: Zhu Mingtao, the director of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Office, believing that the spirit of the security corps in various counties is lax and lacks training, has specially applied to the provincial government to establish a training center for military training instructors of the Zhejiang Provincial County Security Corps.
