Automobile News

Commentary

The Anatomy of the Free Wheel 194

— Dai

▲Unanimous Praise from the British and American Automotive Industries

Articles about the free wheel have been published in this magazine before, so there's no need to repeat them. But today, we will conduct further research for our readers to understand the main advantages of the free wheel and analyze its various benefits. Since the invention of the free wheel, engineers in the British and American automotive industries have generally recognized it as a great success in automobiles and the greatest invention in the history of automobiles. The reason lies in the use of electric power to start the car. When engineers use the free wheel to start a car, it's as if children are riding a bicycle, starting and stopping as they please, very freely. It's truly amazing. In addition, the free wheel has many advantages too numerous to list. Today, we will select the most important points to tell our readers. Taking the Huppmobile as an example, since using the free wheel, one type of six-cylinder car and four types of eight-cylinder straight-edge cars have adopted the free wheel. As a result of using the free wheel in these new cars, test results show that lubricating oil is saved by 18% and gasoline is saved by more than 12%. In addition, the friction of the mechanical parts on the car body is also greatly reduced. This is all because the necessary movement of the clutch can be reduced by 30% to 60% with the use of the free wheel. Moreover, the safety plans adopted by free wheel cars provide drivers with safety and convenience, leaving nothing to be desired.

Free wheel cars can save so much lubricating oil and gasoline because the engines used in the past continued to run even after the throttle was closed, resulting in wasted fuel. Now, except when moving slowly, at 10, 25, or 30 miles per hour, the engine continues to run, but after the throttle is closed, it can stop rotating. Once the free wheel is used on a new car, all vibrations can be completely eliminated. As for rear-end collisions, which are common in ordinary vehicles, they can be avoided in free wheel cars. This is because sudden opening or closing of the throttle can cause shocks to the mechanical parts of ordinary vehicles. Under these circumstances, tire wear can definitely be reduced, as can the wear of the car body. In addition, free wheel cars have another important advantage. Hupp Motor Car Company's various new cars, such as the Century eight-cylinder and six-cylinder new cars, as well as the G, H, and U series new cars, are equipped with free wheels. Even when using second gear, driving is convenient and easy, silent and still.

Taking Hupp Motor Car Company's various new cars equipped with free wheels as an example, their construction principles are quite simple and have no special features. The only difference from ordinary vehicles is that the movement of the clutch in free wheel cars is very convenient. No matter what speed is used, they can move and change each other. This is because in ordinary vehicles, to reduce speed, you must first downshift to a low speed and then shift from low speed to second gear. But free wheel cars are different. Shifting from second gear to the highest speed or from the highest speed to second gear can be done directly, without using the clutch. Under these circumstances, the vehicle's forward momentum will be sufficient to control the engine's forward power. However, if a vehicle does not use a free wheel, gear shifting must require the use of a clutch. This shows that free wheel vehicles are very easy to drive. Therefore, drivers who have used Hupp Motor Car Company's various free wheel new cars are all very satisfied. All movements during driving can be silent, providing drivers with great convenience. Today's automobiles are considered superior if they can operate at the highest speed silently and smoothly. Drivers certainly know this. But since Hupp Motor Car Company introduced free wheel vehicles to society, second gear has also achieved amazing results. This new type of second gear uses a three-part speed method, and its main advantage is silence, and gear changes are even more convenient and easy.

The clutches made in Huppmobile free wheel new cars are of the overrun or one-way type. These clutches allow the vehicle to move forward automatically at about six to eight miles per hour, regardless of whether the gear is the fastest or the next fastest. The clutch operates as if a child is riding a bicycle. For this reason, various Hupp new cars can save gasoline, lubricating oil, and all other expenses when moving, and are more economical. The transmission systems of old-fashioned vehicles are almost regarded as antiques. In crowded places, sometimes when rushing into traffic and starting to drive, free wheel vehicles only need to fully depress the accelerator, and even when the engine stops, the vehicle continues to move forward. Even when driving fast on the road, it is quite convenient to stop the vehicle. The vehicle's own power can also be used to brake. Lowering the accelerator immediately increases the engine speed. Drivers who want to squeeze into the center of traffic in a busy city only need to move the shift lever without touching the clutch to shift to the highest gear. The shift lever only needs to be returned to the third position without touching the clutch. Past results have proven that the movement of the clutch on free wheel cars can be reduced by 30% to 60%. This alone demonstrates the economy of materials and the saving of manpower. Therefore, free wheel new cars can save fuel and reduce the number of repairs, and have been widely welcomed by the automotive industry since their introduction. It is expected that there will be even greater developments soon. We can wait and see.

News

Miscellaneous News on Road Administration in Zhejiang Province 195

— Xue Qian

Zhejiang Province is making rapid progress in road administration, so its achievements are far ahead of other provinces. In the recent month, whether it's separate rectifications, restrictions on fares, surveying routes, or approving the establishment of branch stations, it feels meticulous. Other measures such as revising the license issuance method and urging the payment of road maintenance donations are gradually improving. This cannot be said to be anything other than the result of the attention of the road administration authorities. I will now present the findings of my investigation separately.

▲Separate Rectification of Car Services on the Shaoxing-Xiaoshan Section The Zhejiang Construction Department believes that the highway on the Shaoxing-Xiaoshan section has been quite developed in recent years, but due to the failure to effectively rectify it, road services have gradually deteriorated and passengers feel inconvenienced. Recently, the Shaoxing County Construction Committee proposed to expedite the rectification of road services on the Xiaoshan-Shaoxing section, mainly in three aspects: First, the Road Bureau should extend the ticket window opening hours as appropriate and supervise the road police stationed at the station to maintain order when purchasing tickets. Passengers can line up according to the order of arrival at the station when purchasing tickets, with those arriving first purchasing first, so as to avoid congestion. Second, the Road Bureau should strictly order drivers and station staff to thoroughly inspect the vehicles before each departure. The number of monthly inspections should also be stipulated in peacetime. Once it is discovered that the mechanical parts are slightly damaged, they must be repaired as soon as possible, so that the vehicles will not become irreparable due to minor damage. Third, section cars should be appropriately added depending on the traffic conditions along the route to provide relief. As for the broken car windows and passengers being exposed to wind and rain from time to time, although the matter is small, it greatly affects the people's impression of the Road Bureau and should be repaired as soon as possible to facilitate travel. In addition, it is also appropriate to wash the vehicles and mark the station names. The county has already submitted a request to the Provincial Construction Department to order the Highway Bureau to expedite the rectification of the various aspects in order to improve the situation.

▲Restrictions on Increasing Fares on Various Road Sections The Zhejiang Construction Department recently received a report from the Highway Bureau stating that the prices of various materials have been increasing recently, and the surplus in business revenue has suddenly decreased. It is proposed to slightly increase the fare prices on various road sections to compensate for the losses. A mileage table of various road sections, a table of current fares at various stations, and a table of proposed fare increases in the future were attached to the report. The Construction Department believes that building roads and operating vehicles is originally intended to facilitate transportation, but upon checking the increased fares, many are increased by 70%, and the lowest is also 80% or 90%. The amount seems to be too high, which is not conducive to considering the people's financial capacity. Moreover, most of the vehicles on various road sections are damaged, and passengers feel greatly inconvenienced. The Highway Bureau is strictly ordered to comply with the previous orders and effectively rectify the situation. The proposed fare increase will be reviewed and handled after the rectification is completed and the vehicles on various road sections are replenished.

▲Ningbo Branch Station Postponed Establishment The Ningbo Merchants' Organization Unification Committee and the Fenghua County Merchants' Organization Unification Committee telegraphed the Provincial Highway Bureau, reporting the plan to fill in the moat and add a bus station. A request was submitted to the Provincial Government to quickly order the cancellation of the original proposal in order to facilitate transportation. The Provincial Government then ordered the Provincial Construction Department to investigate and verify the matter and report back. It is recently learned that Shen Guang, the director of the Ningbo-Fenghua Car Service Office appointed by the Highway Bureau, jointly verified the matter with the Ningbo Municipal Government. According to the report, the part of the planned moat filling was originally the wharf for inland waterway vessels in Yin County. If it is filled to be used as a base, the original wharf will inevitably have to be moved westward. As a result, the distance for merchant ships to load and unload goods will be slightly longer, which will inevitably have a slight impact. The local citizens oppose filling the river for this reason. Near the Yuling Bridge Gate, if another station is to be built, there is no suitable location except for the vacant land that the Municipal Government has already put up for auction. Moreover, the value of the vacant land auctioned by the Ningbo Municipal Government is about 25,000 yuan per acre. The current value of funds

Page 20

is depleted, and there is no spare capacity to purchase land for the time being. Therefore, the establishment of the station is proposed to be postponed. The Construction Department, upon receiving the reply, ordered that it be temporarily postponed and ordered the Yin County Magistrate to inform and notify accordingly and report back to the Provincial Government.

▲Surveying of the Songyang-Suichang and Songyang-Lishui Routes Regarding the proposal by the Songyang County Government Construction Section to open and complete the Songyang-Suichang and Songyang-Lishui roads within three years, the Provincial Construction Department previously ordered the Provincial Highway Bureau to send personnel to survey the routes in advance. It was also deemed difficult to approve the proposal to allocate a certain percentage of the county's construction special donation each year as road construction funds. The Songyang County Magistrate was ordered to propose other fundraising methods and submit them for review. It is recently learned that the Highway Bureau has ordered Lu Rui, an assistant engineer from the Huang Le Jian surveying team, to go to survey the routes. The two routes are 185 li long in total and pass through many mountains and cross many large streams. The project is arduous, and the required funds are estimated to be more than 1.3 million yuan. Since these routes are not connected to the Longyou-Xixiao-Changshan Railway, business development is difficult to expect. Engineer Lu also surveyed the Suichang-Longyou section as an attachment. The Provincial Construction Department ordered the Songyang County Magistrate to keep the original report and investigation table for reference. As for the construction costs of the two roads, they must still be handled in accordance with the Construction Department's orders.

▲Revision of the Long-Distance Bus License Issuance Method The Zhejiang Construction Department recently received an order from the Ministry of Railways stating that the regulations for issuing licenses to long-distance bus companies were promulgated by the Ministry on September 5, 1920, and the reporting formats were formulated. A request was submitted to the Executive Yuan for recordation. The Executive Yuan then issued directives No. 2710 and No. 3350, along with the Ministry's previous submission of the revised long-distance bus company license issuance regulations for recordation. The revised long-distance bus company license issuance regulations and formats are hereby copied and distributed for your information. The Construction Department has already revised the long-distance bus company license issuance regulations and formats, copied and distributed them, and notified the county magistrates, the Provincial Highway Bureau, and the various long-distance bus companies operated by merchants.

▲Locomotives Have Been Tested on the Xiaoshan-Changshan Railway Locomotives have been tested on the Xiaoshan-Changshan Railway. Residents along the route flocked to watch. From now on, vehicles will transport materials more frequently. The general public is ignorant of the dangers. A slight carelessness will result in casualties to people and livestock, and the vehicles and roadbeds will also be damaged. For the sake of caution, the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Engineering Bureau listed the items that should be prohibited as follows: (1) Residents along the line should strictly control children and not place stones or other obstacles on the tracks. Violators will be detained. (2) The stone ballast placed on the railway is not allowed to be moved. Violators will be punished. (3) All livestock must not be grazed on the railway. Violators will be heavily fined. (4) The screws, sleepers, and track numbers on the railway are of utmost importance. It is absolutely forbidden to tamper with or steal them. Violators will be ordered to be investigated by the village chief. (5) All ships passing under the railway bridge must proceed slowly. If there is a collision with the piling, the ships should be detained and fined. (6) It is absolutely forbidden for pedestrians to walk on the railway. (7) When pedestrians cross the tracks, they must follow the crosswalks set up by the Road Bureau and pay attention to whether there are trains coming and going. If they hear the whistle, they should immediately move away. It is reported that the Zhejiang Construction Department also believes that this matter concerns the safety of the railway and the people, and has ordered the county to inform the residents of the various villages and neighborhoods along the line not to court disaster.
